No.15 question: Why do I always fail to configure the network?
【response】
code: 0
answer: - Ensure that the device is in a pairing status before network configuration 
- Confirm that the router can be connected to network normally (the phone in the same network can access to the Internet) 
- Check whether the distance from the router is appropriate
- Please check if the device is powered on. For non-HomeBase products, ensure that the Wi-Fi information entered is correct when connecting the device to the network.
- If the issue is still not resolved, please notify our customer service team in this chat window.

No.125 question: Can the video still be recorded when the camera is offline
【response】
code: 0
answer: Hello! Thanks for reaching out.When the camera is offline, if SD card storage (local recording) is being used, it continues to record video. Videos recorded during the offline period can be recovered and viewed after the camera reconnects to the network. If cloud storage (cloud recording) is used, recordings cannot be made over the network while the camera is offline. During the offline period, cloud storage recordings will be paused until the camera reconnects to the network.
uuid: 3e8e9ca0bb2b9994


【request】
uuid: f66e8026-cc61-41be-ad54-e2bc0a81d762
timestamp: 1726222856742
No.126 question: Camera's offline
【response】
code: 0
answer: Thank you for contacting Aosu Technical Support! Kindly follow the steps below to isolate or fix the problem:
1. Check the power source: Ensure the camera is properly connected to a power source and that the power supply is working correctly. If it's a battery camera, ensure that the battery is charged.
2. Check the Wi-Fi connection: Ensure that your Wi-Fi network is stable and that the camera is within range of the router. Move the camera closer to the router or HomeBase to see if it improves the connection.
3. Restart the camera: Try unplugging and re-plugging it from the power source, wait for a few seconds, and try again. This can help refresh the connection.
4. Reconfigure the camera: If the issue persists, you can try resetting the camera to its factory settings. Remove the camera from the app and add it back.
5. Check for firmware updates: Go to Camera settings -> Firmware updates, then Update.

If none of these steps resolve the issue, please provide more details about the problem, such as any error messages you're seeing or specific behavior of the camera when it goes offline. This will help us further investigate the problem for further assistance. Rest assured we will help you sort this out. -Aosu Team
uuid: 9928ee49f3739d3d


【request】
uuid: ecc6a125-ba35-4474-a8d1-33233c5a2c0d
timestamp: 1726222860785

No.132 question: What should I do in case the camera goes offline?
【response】
code: 0
answer: 1. The camera is powered off  
Please connect to a power supply and make sure that the camera at work is always powered on  
2. The camera is placed at an improper position  
Please keep close to the router as possible, and reduce barriers such as walls.  
3. The Wi-Fi name or password has been changed  
Please reconnect in “Settings- Reconnect Wi-Fi”.  
4. The router doesn’t work properly  
Please make sure that the router can be connected to network normally.  
5. The camera is faulty  
Inspect whether the camera is faulty.

【request】
uuid: d6d55fd0-cc40-41ed-ab1f-dd8b6cb7df30
timestamp: 1726222908500
No.147 question: How to install solar panels?
【response】
code: 0
answer: The solar panel must be placed where there is continuous sunlight all the year round. A direct sunlight for several hours a day can suffice for the camera’s power needs.

Note: The solar panel may be susceptible to weather conditions, seasonable change, geographic location and other factors.

1. The provided screws are used to secure the mounting base to the desired position. If the surface of the mounting location is soft, a hole may be drilled on the wall by a φ6.0 bit and with an anchor bolt being inserted, and then the mounting base is secured by screws.
2. First of all, install a screw cap to the universal joint, and then screw the round head nut into the universal joint.
3. Screw the universal joint into the back of the solar panel, and secure it with provided nuts.
4. Screw the tightened screw cap into the mounting base. Make sure that the universal joint faces upward.
5. Adjust the solar panel toward left or right, loosen the screw cap, rotate the screw rod, and then tighten the screw cap after the solar panel is properly installed.
6. The angle of the solar panel may be adjusted upward or downward, even up to 90°.

Note: After installation, please check whether all connections are tight. Keep the solar panel in a mounting angle of 30-45° from the horizontal plane.

Connect the solar panel to the camera, as shown in the picture below (open the silica gel cover at the bottom of the camera, plug the power wire in the USB-C charge port, and then close the cover and loosen the power wire on the solar panel).
uuid: bcfb31a21d2733ea


【request】
uuid: 88d04850-d2cf-49be-9d0a-082eebf182ae
timestamp: 1726222913307
No.148 question: How to install solar panels
【response】
code: 0
answer: The solar panel must be placed where there is continuous sunlight all the year round. A direct sunlight for several hours a day can suffice for the camera’s power needs

Note: The solar panel may be susceptible to weather conditions, seasonable change, geographic location and other factors.

1. The provided screws are used to secure the mounting base to the desired position. If the surface of the mounting location is soft, a hole may be drilled on the wall by a φ6.0 bit and with an anchor bolt being inserted, and then the mounting base is secured by screws.
2. First of all, install a screw cap to the universal joint, and then screw the round head nut into the universal joint.
3. Screw the universal joint into the back of the solar panel, and secure it with provided nuts.
4. Screw the tightened screw cap into the mounting base. Make sure that the universal joint faces upward.
5. Adjust the solar panel toward left or right, loosen the screw cap, rotate the screw rod, and then tighten the screw cap after the solar panel is properly installed.
6. The angle of the solar panel may be adjusted upward or downward, even up to 90°.

Note: After installation, please check whether all connections are tight. Keep the solar panel in a mounting angle of 30-45° from the horizontal plane

Connect the solar panel to the camera, as shown in the picture below (open the silica gel cover at the bottom of the camera, plug the power wire in the USB-C charge port, and then close the cover and loosen the power wire on the solar panel).

No.151 question: How do I choose a country when registering and logging in?
【response】
code: 0
answer: Since different regions correspond to different online servers, you need to select the country where you are when registering and logging in.

For example, if you select the United States when registering, you should also select the United States when you log in to the same account again; if you select another country, it will default to an unregistered account.

No.360 question: How to check why the camera is offline?
【response】
code: 0
answer: 1. The camera is powered off  
Please connect to a power supply and make sure that the camera at work is always powered on  
2. The camera is placed at an improper position  
Please keep close to the router as possible, and reduce barriers such as walls.  
3. The Wi- Fi name or password has been changed  
Please reconnect in “Settings- Reconnect Wi- Fi”.  
4. The router doesn’t work properly  
Please make sure that the router can be connected to network normally.  
5. The camera is faulty  
Inspect whether the camera is faulty.

No.369 question: Does the camera still record video when offline?
【response】
code: 0
answer: Hello! Thanks for reaching out.When the camera is offline, if SD card storage (local recording) is being used, it continues to record video. Videos recorded during the offline period can be recovered and viewed after the camera reconnects to the network. If cloud storage (cloud recording) is used, recordings cannot be made over the network while the camera is offline. During the offline period, cloud storage recordings will be paused until the camera reconnects to the network.

【response】
code: 0
answer: Firmware updates are updates to the software system running on the camera.

Users can also manually check for updates in Camera Settings - Firmware Updates to upgrade.
1. It will take a few minutes to download the installation package, please wait patiently.
2. When updating the firmware, please ensure the camera is powered on and the system running normally.
3. To ensure the using experience and the stability of APP function, please update to the Firmware to the latest version.

No.921 question: How is the battery life of low-power cameras affected by ambient temperature?
【response】
code: 0
answer: The charging efficiency of lithium ion batteries is very low at a temperature below 40°F / 4°C. Therefore, the lithium ion battery used by the camera needs more frequent charging when the temperature is lower than 40°F / 4°C. The battery performance will return to normal once the weather warms and remains above the ice point.
